< Review>
My kids like to come here when they aren't going to Tapioca Express or when we visit Pho 99 or 99 Ranch Market.

Pros: pretty easy to find store, on the corner, free parking, good prices, has a very good menu just like Tapioca Express, foods are very good, drinks also have flavor, not watery, powdery or sugary like some places, portions of food orders is also a plus, prices are good

Cons:  finding parking can be tricky since 99 Ranch Market is there, especially on the weekends, the store is small and only have 3 tables, and could use a cleaning or updating, wait time for food is a bit long,

Egg puff, calamari rings and even the popcorn chicken is great, but don't let it sit in the bag too long or it gets soggy.<//Review>

<GmapID>0x80c2b7020d548fd1:0x5f58667f0257587e</GmapID><name>Lord Flacko<//name><UserId.>100508647605819677114< /UserId.><pictures>None<//pictures><resp>None<//resp></record>

<pictures>None< /pictures><Rating>1< /Rating>< Review>
Where do I begin...
My experience with this dentist was an absolute nightmare.
My experience at "New Smile Dental" caused me deep panic, fear, and pain. For many months after this incident, I was terrified about returning to a dentist again. (Thankfully, I have found a professional, empathetic, and knowledgeable dentist in recent times.)

New Smile Dental should be called New Trauma.

It literally took the dentist--Dr. Michael Dounel-- two days to perform one tooth extraction. I came to this dentist in severe pain, hoping for an emergency extraction of an infected wisdom tooth. He yanked at my mouth as if my mouth was the hood of a car. He was in a hurry and complained bitterly the entire time I was under his "care". When I put my arm up (he told me to raise my arm to signal if I was in pain), he would angrily yell at me to put my arm down. He denied that I was in pain and several times, despite my groaning, told me I was "just fine" and that "he'd given me more than enough pain relief."

I gripped the seat, my hands dripping in sweat, hoping this man would not pull too hard and cause irreparable damage.

At one point, frustrated with my cries for help, he said, "I'm a dentist, not a magician."

This man is definitely not a magician. I cannot even say he is a dentist.

He was rude, cold, and very harsh. He has terrible bedside manner.

I literally ran out of the office as soon as he was finished with me. I was in even more pain then when I entered his office.

The worst part?

Even in his impatience, he still had not managed to complete the job.

I had to return the very next day to go through even more harsh treatment.

I have had all my wisdom teeth removed at a different dentist office. This new dentist was deeply perplexed at the work Dr. Dounel had done and looked at my mouth in shock. He told me I should never have had this man perform this sort of extraction. I only wish I knew this sooner. This new dentist also warned me to never to go back to New Smile. I assured him that I would never go back to Dr. Dounel--even if someone paid me.

I write this a year out  from my terrible experience because it has taken me this long to process this  painful experience. I write this review to help others. I truly do not believe the many five star reviews of New Smile to be real. Please scroll down to read other less favorable reviews and you will see a more truthful picture of Dr. Dounel emerge. He blames customers who give him lower ratings and cannot take accountability for his actions. This man has little empathy for people in pain. He is insensitive, arrogant, and forever in a hurry.

I do wonder if his treatment of me was racially and/or economically motivated, and I cannot recommend his services for any Black or Brown person (no matter how many staged pictures he posts of his diverse clientele...). Please go elsewhere if you are searching for competent, sympathetic care. And DO NOT have your teeth extracted at this office.

Best of luck to any and all who read this. I release the pain this experience caused me and I hope this review helps others. I am so thankful I survived this ordeal and that I had such great service at a different office.

Take good care and God bless</Review>

I've been coming here for two years now and I think it's past due for a review. I was looking for a barber shop when I first moved here and found this place close to my house. It's tucked into the back corner of the Albertson's parking lots next to Brian's BBQ.
I generally see Clint for my haircut but I've gotten my hair cut by all the guys and they do a great job. Clint has got the style I'm going for down; I barely tell him anything and he gets it exactly right.
They do a lot of fades and old school style cuts, straight razor shave to clean the edges and style up your hair so you look fresh. I also buy all my pomade here since they have a good selection.

Dig this: Today, Sunday Aug. 30, 2020 , my first time to JB on Myrtle in Monrovia. It was 90 degrees and I walked back to the shop to get more Avacado Sauce and they wanted $1.00. I said no I will return the food.
Beware everyone only enough sauce for 1/2 a taquito.
So I return the food get my $10.20 back.
I think they should give a large sauce for the taquitos in the first place.
SO, the point is: Instead of giving me the large Avacado sauce for free, they refunded my whole order and I went across the street to eat.
Maybe, just maybe it would of been wise to give me the sauce which was probably a cost of 3 cents or (five) 5 cents, a nickel.
Instead it made more sense to the ladies to refund my full order of $10.20 over 3-5 cents.
Just sayin....<//review>
